Despair for Puppet Organization's Participation in Far Eastern Games Performance

Our Country Refutes Japan with Reason　Philippines Argues to Act According to Bylaws, Japan at a Loss for Words　Japan Proposes Postponement of This Far Eastern Games, Decision to Be Made by Philippines　Japanese Athletic Association Unreasonably Scolds Filipinos

The 10th Far Eastern Games have fallen into a trend of indefinite postponement. The result of the informal meeting yesterday morning at the Cathay Hotel between representatives of China, Japan, and the Philippines was that China and Japan each held fast to their own opinions, not yielding in the slightest regarding the participation of the puppet organization, thus forming a deadlock with no results. Finally, the Japanese representative proposed postponing this session of the Games. Dr. Tan, the Philippine representative, also returned to the Philippines yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM on the Empress of Asia. Dr. Tan agreed to telegraph China and Japan in the near future regarding whether the Philippines agrees to the postponement. The Japanese representative had high hopes beforehand, believing that with the assistance of the Philippine representative, they would return victoriously. Now that the result is like this, they are greatly dissatisfied. The details of yesterday's meeting are compiled as follows:

Cathay Hotel Meeting Continues

Chinese, Japanese, and Philippine representatives continued to hold an informal meeting at 9:05 AM yesterday morning in Room 523 of the Cathay Hotel on Nanjing Road to discuss the issue of the puppet organization's participation in the Far Eastern Games performance. The attending representatives were the same as the day before: Cao Yunxiang, director of the Chinese Olympic Committee, and Shen Siliang, key member of the Chinese Olympic Committee, representing China; Yamamoto, Matsuzawa, and Qian Jingmo, the consul stationed in Shanghai, representing Japan; and Dr. Tan and secretaries Zhou Jiaqi and Ms. Li, representing the Philippines. With Dr. Tan as chairman, the records from the previous day were first exchanged, amended, reviewed, and finalized, and then the debate began on the puppet organization participation issue, which has garnered global attention. The atmosphere was tense, and the Chinese and Japanese representatives insisted on their respective positions. Until 11:30 AM at noon, there were still no results, and the meeting was adjourned.

Wrangling Over Words, Attempting to Be Sophistical

The focus of yesterday's meeting was on finding a possible way to resolve this issue. The Japanese representative still insisted on the precedent of India's participation in the 1930 performance, wrangling over the records of the previous session and the wording of the conference bylaws to put up a strong argument. The focus of the issue was on unanimous consent versus majority consent. The Japanese side claimed that India's participation in the 1930 performance was not agreed upon by all members, but was only proposed by the Philippines and supported by China. Therefore, the participation of the puppet organization this time only requires a proposal from Japan and support from the Philippines, and a majority can pass it, because the records at that time did not specify unanimous consent. Thereupon, the Chinese representative refuted the Japanese side's sophistry, saying that although the records did not specify unanimous passage for India's participation in the performance, they also did not specify Japan's opposition. In other words, it was unanimously passed without any doubt. The Japanese representative had no response.

Exhausted Reason and Words, At Wit's End

The debate between the two sides was very intense. The Japanese side especially often based its sophistry on extremely minor standpoints. However, its words were clumsy, and its reasons were non-existent, and it was repeatedly refuted by our side. Our representative even asked that, according to their intention, if the inclusion of the puppet organization has nothing to do with politics, why did they not submit it to the General Assembly themselves, and why did they have to ask your country to act as a proxy? The Japanese person was at a loss for words and reason, and the awkwardness of being at wit's end was obvious. Then the Japanese person went on to say that if China acknowledges the inclusion of the puppet organization, even if it does not actually participate, it will not be impossible. This is enough to show their desperate and ugly state.

All Three Methods Overturned

The two sides moved to extremes, so with overall agreement, several possible solutions were drafted. There were three methods: (1) To temporarily not discuss this issue and submit it to the General Assembly in Manila for discussion, meaning the puppet organization cannot participate in this session and its participation in the next session would be decided at the Manila General Assembly, but as a result of the vote, Japan cast a negative vote, so it did not pass. (2) To submit this issue to the Executive Committee for discussion. As a result of the vote, Japan also opposed it, because it was certain that it would be opposed by our country's committee member Wang Zhengting without a doubt. The last (3rd) method was to temporarily follow Japan's proposal to vote by majority, and immediately ask the Philippines to express its decision on whether it is possible. If the Philippines agrees, then our country would withdraw; if the Philippines opposes, then Japan would succumb or withdraw. It could be decided with a single word, but the Philippine representative opposed it, unwilling to vote for agreement or disagreement, saying that the Philippines' actions must be based on the conference bylaws and cannot be taken rashly. The three methods having been successively overturned, the meeting fell into a state of no result.

Unable to Salvage, Meeting Adjourned

The Philippine representative, unable to decide at this point, seeing that both sides were insisting very strongly, decided not to put it to a vote and was unable to salvage the situation, so the meeting was adjourned. Dr. Tan said in his address that since both China and Japan held their own opinions, and the conference records were incomplete (referring to the 1930 India issue), and limited by the regulations of the conference bylaws, the decision on this issue would not be put to a vote, and the Chinese and Japanese sides would be allowed to resolve it however they wish. But in the worst case, if the Far Eastern Games were to be dissolved, the Philippines is prepared to make such a sacrifice. However, what must be told to China and Japan is that the Philippines has spent tens of millions in the preparations for this Far Eastern Games, building sports fields, etc., which is quite a large amount. The last wish is that China and Japan can cooperate, as in previous sessions.

Japanese Side Proposes Postponement of Far Eastern Games

The Japanese representative then stood up and proposed to the Philippine representative to postpone this session of the Games. The Philippine representative replied that this issue would have to wait until after discussions upon returning to the Philippines before it could be answered. Once the decision is made upon returning to the Philippines, China and Japan will be immediately notified by telegram. The representatives of the three countries had no different opinions. The Chinese and Japanese representatives thanked Dr. Tan, the Philippine representative, for coming all the way to Shanghai to chair the meeting, and then the meeting was adjourned.

Philippine Representative Left Shanghai Yesterday

Philippine representative Dr. Tan, seeing the deteriorating situation of yesterday's meeting and that the opinions of China and Japan were moving to extremes, unable to be salvaged, and also because the Philippine side was in the position of host, it was difficult to express an opinion, so after the meeting ended, he took the Changxing Company's Empress of Asia ship from Shanghai at 4:00 PM in the afternoon to return to the Philippines to report the course of events to the various preparation authorities of the Far Eastern Games. Shen Siliang and others from the Chinese Olympic Committee all went to the pier to see him off. Observing the current situation, the future of the Far Eastern Games scheduled to be held in the Philippines on May 12 is difficult to predict because the Japanese side's proposal for the puppet organization to participate in the performance is affecting the future of the Games. The Games will be postponed indefinitely. It is heard that the Philippine side has already spent five million yuan on the preparations for this session of the Games.

Far Eastern Games Pre-Selection Continues

According to Shen Siliang, although the future of the Far Eastern Games is still unknown, the various pre-selection procedures will definitely continue to be held. Today is the last day for various places to register to participate in the pre-selection. Famous athletes in this city have all registered. The pre-selection will still proceed according to the original plan. As for whether the Games will be held, we will let it take its course.

Japan Bears the Blame for the Breakdown of the Far Eastern Games

According to Shen Siliang, there are many misunderstandings among the people of the country regarding the Far Eastern Games issue. In fact, our authorities have been actively fighting at all times. Because this meeting was of an informal nature and related to international face, it was necessary to participate in the discussions. However, we were determined to deal with it with justice. If it reaches a point where it cannot be salvaged, we will naturally withdraw in order to implement our past statements. We will never dare to act arbitrarily, so as to harm the national dignity. All future matters must wait for the Philippine side to express their opinion. In short, our positions and those of Japan are moving to extremes. If the Japanese side insists on not yielding, then the Games will break down, or our country will withdraw, and the blame should be borne by the Japanese side.

Two Track and Field Teams Issue Declaration

The Beijing Zhonghua and Shanghai Baihong track and field teams issued a declaration yesterday, saying, "To the public of the national sports community, now, a certain country instigates the puppet Manchukuo to participate in the Far Eastern Games, intending to create our country's tacit recognition of the formal existence of the puppet Manchukuo. This is using the name of sports to help its aggression. If we shamelessly stand shoulder to shoulder with the puppet Manchukuo on the field, the issue of the puppet Manchukuo, which is not recognized by the League of Nations, the countries of the world, and our national populace, will be lightly sacrificed by our sports community. Although yesterday's meeting had no results, the three methods drafted by the Philippine side were not in our favor. It is hoped that our sports community will unite and rise up so that the authorities can have a solid backing, preferring to withdraw from the Far Eastern Games rather than yield even slightly. Beijing Zhonghua Track and Field Team, Shanghai Baihong Track and Field Team, respectfully."

Japan Actually Complains About the Philippines

According to yesterday's Japanese newspaper Shanghai Mainichi, at the special meeting of the Second Far Eastern Games, the claims of Japan and China are still far apart. Before convening this meeting, the Philippines originally agreed with Japan's claim, but unexpectedly, its attitude changed greatly at the meeting, actually leaning towards the Chinese side. It avoided making a decision on the current issue, and did its best to delay, thereby rejecting the majority claim of the Japanese side, and agreeing with China's claim of unanimous agreement. Japan's proposal therefore failed, it is said.

Official Meeting Records

Far Eastern Games Standing Committee Meeting Records, exchanged, amended, reviewed, and published on April 10.

▲Ninth Day Records A meeting was held at 10:00 AM on the morning of the ninth at the Shanghai Shenyuan Football Field office. Attending representatives were Dr. Tan (Philippine representative and chairman), Cao Yunxiang (China), Shen Siliang (China), Yamamoto (Japan), Matsuzawa (Japan), Qian Jingmo (Japan). The five motions have been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. ▲Ninth Day Afternoon Records Attending representatives and location were the same as above. The meeting was held at 2:30 PM. Informal discussion of the Manchuria participation issue The Japanese representative cited the example of India's participation in the 1930 performance, stating that the issue of Manchuria's participation in this session of the Games is of a performance nature, not joining as a member. According to Articles 3 and 10 of the conference bylaws, the Chinese representative stated that there is no need to discuss the issue of Manchuria's participation. The Japanese representative stated that the acceptance or non-acceptance of Manchuria's participation in the performance only requires passage by a majority of members, not unanimous passage. The Japanese representative stated that the case of accepting India's participation in the performance was not specially noted in the records at the time, and it is thought that it was passed by a majority, not by all. The Chinese representative stated that because there were no dissenting opinions in the General Assembly at that time, it was considered that the case was passed by the entire General Assembly. The Chinese representative stated that it did not agree with the Japanese side's opinion, and therefore proposed that it be submitted to the next General Assembly for discussion. The Philippine representative stated that the Philippines welcomes any new units to participate in the competition, but when sending a letter to Manchuria, it was stated that it should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Articles 3 and 10 of the conference bylaws. The Chinese representative stated that now the Chinese and Japanese sides each hold their own views on this issue, and there is no need to continue the discussion. The Japanese representative proposed that discussion of this issue should be given sufficient time for consideration by all parties, and that the meeting should be rescheduled. The chairman accepted the Japanese representative's proposal and asked the representatives to reconvene at the Cathay Hotel at 9:15 AM tomorrow morning. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM. ▲Tenth Day Records Location: Cathay Hotel, Time: 9:15 AM. Attendees were the same as the ninth day. Chairman: Dr. Tan. The meeting was convened to amend and pass the ninth day's records, sending one copy to each country. All agreed. After informally drafting possible solutions to the Manchuria participation issue, it was discussed again. (1) To submit the issue to the next General Assembly for discussion. (2) In accordance with the provisions of Article 14 of the conference bylaws, to immediately submit the issue to the Executive Committee for resolution. (3) According to the Japanese side's rebuttal (participation in the performance only requires passage by a majority), to immediately ask the Philippines to give a definite indication of whether it is possible, in order to resolve the issue. Although the above three methods have undergone informal voting, there is still no satisfactory result. The chairman, observing from the attitudes of the Chinese and Japanese sides each holding their own opinions, and the provisions of Articles 3 and 10 of the conference bylaws, and the incomplete records of the India participation issue in the records, has caused the opinions between China and Japan to move to extremes. This representative (Philippines) will temporarily not vote on this issue, but will only listen to the current members to make a final solution. However, the Philippines has been preparing for this session of the Games for a long time, and of course sincerely hopes that the countries can maintain their past spirit and give the host country appropriate cooperation. The Japanese representative proposed to reschedule this session of the Far Eastern Games in order to give the countries a further opportunity to consider the issue, and to avoid the unpleasant image of having a meeting or before the meeting. The Philippine representative is willing to convey the Japanese side's proposal to the officials of the Philippine Olympic Committee, and the final decision will be telegraphed to China and Japan in the near future. The Chinese and Japanese representatives expressed their gratitude to Dr. Tan for his work as chairman of this meeting. The meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM. ▲Appendix Translation of Far Eastern Games Bylaws The following are three articles of the Far Eastern Games Bylaws: (Article 3) Countries within the Far Eastern region may join as formal members at any time and have the qualifications of attending representatives, but must be formally approved by all members of the General Assembly. (Article 10) Competition qualifications: (A) The Far Eastern Championships are competitions for amateur athletes from the member countries of the Far Eastern Games. Nationals residing abroad may also represent their home country to attend the competition. (B) Those who have represented a country in any international competition may not represent other countries to attend the Far Eastern Games. (C) Each member shall be directly and fully responsible for the amateur qualifications of its representatives and shall comply with the amateur sports rules described below. (Article 14) Appendix: These bylaws may be amended with the consent of two-thirds of the members of the General Assembly or the passage of the entire Executive Committee.

Japan Prepares　to Stop Participating in Far Eastern Games　At a Loss for Words and Reason, Scolding Filipinos Instead

▲Regarding this meeting, Japan had extremely high hopes beforehand, but unexpectedly, things went against its wishes and it was at a loss. However, it still does not blame its own lack of words and reason, but instead complains about the Filipinos' lack of assistance, scolding the Philippines for not keeping its promise, which is quite strange. Now, a telegram from Tokyo says that Japan is preparing to stop participating in this session of the Far Eastern Games, which is also recorded below.

Emergency Board Meeting of the Japanese Athletic Association (Japan Allied Press Tokyo, 10th) The Japanese Athletic Association convened an emergency board meeting, and as a result, at 3:00 PM in the afternoon, sent a telegram to Dr. Yamamoto as follows:

"The meeting is hopeless, we have learned. Colleagues are extremely indignant. The reason why Japan has been striving to participate until now is to show good faith to the Philippines. The Filipinos' attitude of disregarding good faith has been made clear. Without waiting for your return to the country, regarding whether or not to participate in the Games, the board of directors believes that it is necessary to make a major decision. Please report the fact of the Filipinos' breach of faith in detail. Signed, Ping Yanting San, Vice Chairman."

▲Preparation to Stop Participating in the Far Eastern Games (Japan Allied Press Tokyo, 10th) The Japanese Athletic Association convened an emergency board meeting this afternoon (10th). In view of the results of the Shanghai round table meeting, the participation in the Far Eastern Games has become doubtful. Except for the athletes who should continue to train, all other preparations have been suspended. At the same time, this intention will be notified to all parties, it is said.

Philippine Island Announces　Postponement, No Later Than This Year　Refusal of Puppet Country Not the Main Reason

(National News Agency, Manila, 10th) It is reported that the Far Eastern Games will likely be postponed. It is rumored that it was stalled because the puppet Manchukuo's request to participate was rejected. Today, Bagga, Vice President of the Philippine Amateur Athletic Association, denied this, saying that the puppet country's participation is not the main reason for the postponement. In fact, the national athlete teams are all rushed for time and unable to prepare all the procedures for attending the meeting. As for the date of the meeting, it will be announced after it is determined by the President of the Far Eastern Games, probably no later than this year, it is said.

Filipinos in Philippines　All Indignant

(National News Agency, Manila, 9th) The Philippine Chinese General Chamber of Commerce and the Manila Chinese Daily Newspaper Association held a meeting today and resolved that if the puppet Manchukuo is allowed to join the Far Eastern Games, China must refuse to participate in the Far Eastern Games. It is rumored that the puppet country has been approved to send a team to participate. If the Chinese athlete team joins the competition together with the puppet country's athletes, the Filipinos have decided not to entertain the Chinese athletes. A famous local newspaper today published a full-page editorial, stating that in today's situation, if the Chinese athlete team comes with the puppet Manchukuo athletes, then these people are directly selling out the country. The local Chinese community is paying close attention to the news of the round table meetings held in Shanghai in recent days by representatives of China, the Philippines, Japan, and the puppet. Each newspaper publishes an extra edition as soon as it gets new developments, it is said.

Wang Zhengting　Expresses a Firm Attitude　▲Rather Withdraw▲Than Succumb

(Beiping, 10th) Wang Zhengting, the chief representative of Ping to participate in the Far Eastern Games, said that Japan's proposal for the puppet organization to participate in the Far Eastern Games has no basis or reason. Because the Far Eastern Games regulations state that any new unit participating in the Far Eastern Games must be agreed upon by the other countries. If we do not recognize the issue of the puppet organization's participation, it will be difficult to become a reality. Moreover, the issue between the puppet organization countries has not been recognized and is not worth deep concern. If Japan forces its participation, we will definitely withdraw to show resistance. I will go to Shanghai on the 11th to prepare for the pre-selection.

Wu Yunrui　Talks About Japan's Unreasonableness

(Central, Nanjing, 10th) Wu Yunrui said that Japan's proposal at the round table meeting for the puppet organization to participate in the Far Eastern Games as a non-member, and using India's participation as an example, is unreasonable. The Northeast is our territory, which is different from India. How can the people of our country be separated from our country and participate? If the meeting has no results, we would rather withdraw and hold a sports meeting while the national athletes are in Shanghai.

Japanese Baseball Team Selection Decided　Assembled from the Elite of Tokyo's Six Universities

(Japan Allied Press, Tokyo, 10th) The Tokyo Universities Baseball Committee considered the selection of the Japanese baseball representatives for the Far Eastern Games on the 9th. As a result, it was decided to select outstanding athletes from the six universities to form a united army as the Japanese representatives. Diligent Athletics Monthly, Issue 7, Published

▲ Many Articles Severely Criticize

The "Diligent Athletics Monthly," compiled and published by the Diligent Bookstore at 392 Rue Labourdonnais, Shanghai, a groundbreaking publication in the athletic world, has released its seventh issue today. The content of this issue is extremely rich. The cover features a healthy and beautiful photograph of Ms. Li Yuanfen, who set a national record for the women's long jump, which is quite valuable. The pictorial section includes "The Chinese Women's Championship Team in the Shanghai International Basketball Tournament," "Slow and Beautiful Poses in Gymnastics," "The German National Sports Festival," "Cross-Country Running Popular in Europe," "Panoramic View of the Far Eastern Games Venue," and "Hungarian Dance," totaling thirty images. In addition to the "Editor's Note," the textual content includes Shao Rugan's "Looking Forward to the Far Eastern Games and Rejecting the Participation of the Puppet Manchukuo," Yuan Chi's "Our Country's Delay in Preparing for the Far Eastern Games Preliminary," Su Min's "Thoughts on Superintendent Hao's Report on Inspecting Various Athletic Schools," and Yan Shunhua's "The Athletic World Should Cooperate Together," among others. The special articles include Wang Jianwu's "Middle School Athletics," Sun Hanhua's "The Direction Chinese Athletics Should Take," Wei Cen's "Women's Athletics and Physiological Changes," Tao Zhi's "High-Heeled Leather Shoes Hinder Women's Posture," Jin Yiming's "A New Interpretation of the Yijin Jing," Hao Gengsheng's "Report on Inspecting Various Athletic Schools in Shanghai," and Liu Changchun's "Hopes for the Comrades Attending the Far Eastern Games," totaling seven articles. The training section includes Ruan Weicun's "New Techniques in Track and Field" and Yu Zizhen's "Guidance Methods for Children's Track and Field." The teaching materials include Ruan Weicun's "Hungarian Dance" and Cai Yanbin's "Local Game Teaching Materials." The reader's circle includes Liu Shenzhan's "Impressions and Criticisms of the Diligent Athletics Monthly" and Tian Yongqing's "The Necessary Understanding of Athletics," totaling two articles. The records include "Preparation Status of the Sino-Japanese-Philippine Far Eastern Games," "Athletic Administration in the Past Month," "Sports Competitions," "Athletic Personnel," "Overseas Athletics," "National Track and Field Swimming Highest Records," and news from the Ministry of Education's Athletic Class Alumni Association, totaling seven articles. The price is 20 cents per issue, and the annual subscription for twelve issues is 2 dollars and 40 cents. Domestic postage is 18 cents extra, and foreign postage is 1 dollar and 80 cents extra. Currently, the bookstore is promoting athletics by offering an annual subscription for twelve issues for only 2 dollars, with no domestic postage and an additional 80 cents for foreign postage. It is said that this monthly publication is well-edited and beautifully illustrated, so it is popular throughout the country. During this season of spring sunshine and athletic activities, the demand from all parties is exceptionally high, and subscriptions are even more enthusiastic. More than 7,000 schools above the middle school level across the country have subscribed, and there are 6,715 social education institutions across the country that have subscribed. The remaining individual subscriptions are also over 5,000. In this city, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education has issued a notice to all schools and social education institutions to adopt it uniformly, which shows the reputation of the newspaper and the needs of the athletic and educational circles across the country. The bookstore's retail department at 277 Sima Road also sells it at the same price.

Education News

Zhou Hou Shu Discusses His Impressions of Educational Observation in Japan ㈠

▲ Japanese Teaching of Knowledge and Skills Mostly Aims at Foreign Expansion and Aggression Against China

▲ Educational Policy Has Always Consistently Emphasized Physical Fitness Training, Military Training, and Labor Production

I and others were sent by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education to Japan to observe education. We departed from Shanghai at the end of February and returned home this time, spending a total of six weeks in Japan. We stayed in Tokyo for about three weeks and visited Yokohama, Nagoya, Bikai County, Kyoto, Osaka, Nara, Kobe, Beppu, Nagasaki, and other places for about three weeks. During these six weeks, we visited and inquired at educational administrative organizations, observed universities, higher education institutions, specialized schools, middle schools, normal schools, elementary schools, higher elementary vocational schools, social education organizations, social welfare organizations, factories, farms, and rural enterprise organizations, totaling more than eighty locations. The initial draft of the group observation report will be organized and completed soon, and we plan to submit it to the Provincial Department of Education. In the future, we also plan to publish it in a special volume. During our visits in Japan, we were often stimulated by the arrogance of their imperialist spirit, which we can never forget. We also hope to share this with various sectors in our country to strengthen our spirit of unity and resistance against aggression.

Japanese education explicitly takes loyalty to the emperor and love of country as its main purpose, but in reality, it encourages all the young citizens of the country to be brave and fierce and makes them firmly believe in aggressive nationalism. The teaching of all knowledge and skills is mostly aimed at foreign expansion, especially aggression against China. This should be something that we deeply pay attention to and strive to be vigilant about. The general young citizens have received such education, and after they grow up in the future, their ferocity of mind and viciousness of behavior towards China can be imagined. It is truly chilling. The most frightening thing is that the general principals and hosts, while making it their business to instill in their young citizens the idea of foreign aggression, all try their best to express their friendly attitude when we visit. Some even say that Japan's behavior towards China is the fault of the warlords and has nothing to do with the educational community. They are full of honeyed words and concealed daggers, and it is quite difficult to defend their claims. The Japanese educational community absolutely obeys the government, and the government is entirely controlled by the warlords. Saying that it has nothing to do with it is really incomprehensible. When the Japanese are occupying the four northeastern provinces, attempting to include my five northern provinces in their bag, and vigorously implementing economic and political aggression, their government is still deceiving the world's powers and the entire country, up and down, with the high-sounding tone of Sino-Japanese friendship. Now, looking at the words and attitudes of the educational community and even the general public, they are all in line with the government. From this, we can see their national unity and national diplomacy spirit. Recently, I have heard that various sectors in our country have successively organized Japanese visiting groups. I hope that when accepting the Japanese's courteous treatment, generous hospitality, and sweet words, do not be misled. More importantly, do not forget that they are our great enemies that we will never forget. The sweeter their words, the more suspicious their intentions are. I hope you do not neglect this.

The absurdity of Japan's educational purpose, viewed from the perspective of our country's broad Three Principles of the People, should not only be regarded as our great enemy but also as the world's public enemy. Although its purpose is not worth taking, there are many aspects of its implementation that are worth emulating. This is what we paid special attention to during our observation. Now, based on my personal observations, I will briefly list several of its advantages as follows:

㈠ Educational Policy is Consistent From Beginning to End

Japanese education values conservatism and has few changes. After Westernization, the Imperial Rescript on Education was promulgated in the 23rd year of Meiji (1890), which mainly focused on filial piety, fraternal love, loyalty, trustworthiness, cultivating learning, advancing in virtue, loving the country, and being loyal to the emperor. For decades, the whole country has adhered to it without wavering. On the one hand, it takes it as its duty to educate everyone. According to its Ministry of Education, the number of literate people in the country reaches 99.51% of the total population. On the other hand, the entire educational community in the country adopts the same pace from beginning to end. Therefore, although all policies and methods are not new, they are consistent from top to bottom. Having been implemented for a long time, the effectiveness is naturally visible. Our country's educational community has never had a spirit of independence, plagiarizing from the East and the West, each acting on its own, creating new things, and being fickle. Since the implementation of new education, it has also been ten years. In terms of time, it is not later than Japan, but because the direction and policies are not uniform throughout the country and are not consistent from beginning to end, there is still nothing to be accomplished. The level of education of the people has instead declined. Therefore, if our country's education does not want to seek progress, it is fine, but if it wants to seek progress, it should implement centralization. The government should establish a simple policy that is suitable for the national conditions and order the whole country to follow it uniformly. Those who violate it should be subject to the law. Once the policy is set and the steps are unified, foreign academic thoughts can only be attached to this central idea and cannot fundamentally shake it. If this is done for a long time, the effect will be considerable.

㈡ Emphasize Physical Fitness Training

The emphasis on physical fitness training in Japanese schools and society is truly astonishing. The students' regular physical education is not like our country's, which is completely dominated by ball games. Ball sports are generally good, but they are not easy to popularize. Students who do not like sports often stand by and watch or escape to the self-study room to bury themselves in books. Japanese physical education emphasizes generalized sports. When we observed physical education classes in primary and secondary schools, the boys did a whole hour of stretching exercises, gymnastics, vaulting horse, rope climbing, jumping exercises, etc., without interruption. The girls did regular and artistic dance exercises. Every morning, there is an extremely orderly and vigorous morning exercise. After class, there are kendo, judo, archery, wrestling, and other wrestling sports. In the summer, there is swimming, and during vacations, there are seaside activities for the coastal groups and mountain climbing excursions for the mountain groups. Usually, teachers lead them on walking trips of dozens or hundreds of miles. In addition to emphasizing physical fitness training, schools also pay attention to nutrition and hygiene. For example, at Tokyo Municipal No. 1 Middle School, students must have lunch at school, and the school provides the necessary nutritious food for young people. This is actually neglected by the general education community and should be paid attention to. As for the promotion of various sports competitions in society, it is even more universally and enthusiastically seen everywhere. The radio broadcasts a morning exercise program at 7 a.m., so that people across the country can follow along. The rest of the time is mostly broadcasting news of competitions on the sports field. From this, it can be seen that the sports fields everywhere are full of space and time all day long, and it can also be seen that the general public likes and admires this.

Jiangsu Educational Observation Delegation Returns

Zhou Shu (head of the delegation), principal of Yangzhou Middle School; Cao Chu, principal of Zhenjiang Normal School; Yan Liyang, principal of Xuzhou Middle School; Teng Songshi, principal of Huangdu Rural Normal School; Zhao Fengqian, curator of the Zhenjiang Mass Education Center; Liu Jian of the Zhenjiang County Education Bureau; and Yu Jiwen, a teacher at Zhenjiang Normal School, of the Jiangsu Provincial Educational Observation Delegation, took the Empress of Asia from Nagasaki on April 8 and arrived in Shanghai on the morning of the 10th. After the observation was completed, they immediately returned to the Provincial Department to report their findings. Shen Shanzhi, principal of Shanghai Middle School Elementary School and principal of the Normal School Affiliated Elementary School of Sheng Lang, returned to the country one day earlier.

Starting from the 23rd Year, the Central Government Will Allocate 50,000 Yuan Monthly for Pingjiao (Equal Education) Funds

(Nanjing, 10th) The central government cooperated with the educational funding of Beiping City. Previously, due to the depletion of the national treasury, it had been reduced. Now it has been decided that, starting from the first semester of the 23rd year, 50,000 yuan will be allocated monthly.

Hunan Provincial Department of Education Rewards Specialist Students from This Province, 105 Yuan Each

(Changsha, 10th) The Provincial Department of Education has selected 100 Hunan students specializing inside and outside the province, giving each a reward of 105 yuan.

Hongying Library Actively Prepares, Trial Opening This Autumn, the Question of Building a Library Still Needs to be Considered

The Hongying Library was established with funds donated by industrialist Ye Hongying to inherit the books of the Renwen Library. A preparatory office is currently set up on Avenue Joffre. It is actively preparing and plans to open on a trial basis in the autumn. The question of building a library has not yet been decided. The details are as follows:

Trial Opening This Autumn

After the library's preparatory office moved to its new address on Avenue Joffre, it was considered that the environment there was beautiful and the building was spacious, and it was planned to open on a trial basis this autumn. However, since a large part of the library's collection of historical tests and other books has not yet been cataloged, and it is difficult for the existing staff to cope with the workload, it is feared that the opening will not be possible in the autumn. Therefore, it is actively working and will try to increase personnel as much as possible to assist in the handling, hoping to open on time as scheduled.

The Question of Building a Library Still Needs to be Considered

The library originally planned to purchase land in a suitable location in the French Concession to build a new library building. However, since the library's fund is currently only 40 yuan, and the cost of purchasing land, building, and equipment is included, the monthly expenses have been more than 2,000 yuan. If a part of the fund is used, the remaining interest will be used to cover daily expenses, which may not be enough to allocate. Therefore, the question of building a library building still needs to be carefully considered before a decision can be made.

Drifting Fragrance of the Imperial Incense

— Translated by Qin Shouou

But the journey from Beijing to Fengtian was indeed too far, even the Empress Dowager herself knew she could no longer travel by imperial carriage. And she had happened to buy a "royal train" from a foreign railway company. Although she had spent an astonishing amount of money on it—this wasn't because the people at the railway company were deceiving her, but because everyone involved in the transaction wanted money, layer upon layer, until finally, the total was enough to cover the entire annual expenditure of a small country. Li Lianying, of course, also had a share; no one knows how much silver he got. But she hadn't even used it once yet. She often wondered... what it would be like to ride a train, so this time, she was determined to try it out. It was really rare for her to leave Beijing City. Taking this opportunity to go to Fengtian, she wanted to see the land she ruled; perhaps she even wanted to see a few commoners, but this was, in fact, impossible. Because ordinary commoners were not allowed to see her as a rule, and so she couldn't see them. Whenever the imperial carriage went on tour, not only were idlers not allowed to linger on the main streets, but even pedestrians on the nearby side streets were sure to be driven away. However, as my sister and I knew, whenever the Empress Dowager or the Emperor passed by on the street, there was no resident on either side who didn't poke a hole in their paper window and peek out from it; but because the imperial carriages and the red sedan chairs of the court ladies were all sealed tight, even though they were peeking from the window holes, they couldn't see so much as one of our hands or feet. I often liked to pull open my sedan chair curtain a little, so as to see the scenery outside, but I didn't dare pull it open too much, so that people outside could see me; because if I were so informal, others would greatly criticize me. Spring and Autumn: The City in Spring

— Huang Kewei

Spring, a charming season. On the asphalt streets, the newly green street trees release their fresh fragrance; the trams carry patches of shade, lumbering along like drunken men, trudging forward with staggering steps.

The wind blowing from the Huangpu River is gentle, opening up the hearts of everyone! The girls have changed into bright and beautiful fashions, and like newborn swallows, they shyly hold the arms of their young lovers, lightly drifting into the intoxicating park. In the bright sunshine, on the soft grass, the shadows of lovers are reflected; on the red benches, in the dark green shade, the fragrance of flesh and the fragrance of powder are scattered, and amorous words are spoken. At the edge of the broad green leaves of the palm trees, the red cheeks of the girls are revealed, like bright red Flag apples in the green basins of a confectionery shop; laughter and fragrant breath boil over, and the public park of spring has returned to its golden age.

The faces of the people are all adorned with traces of joyous smiles, only the lonely young man, using the walking stick hung on his arm as a lover, and the old gardener who has lost his charm as a loved one, wanders in solitude on the gloomy riverbank, in the secluded thickets, looking at the rippling surface of the river, and listening to the clear singing of the orioles, like a melancholy poet.

When the black net of night is spread out, young men and women in the throes of springtime, as if drunk or enchanted, drill into the dance halls rippling with the light of spring! The passion of youth burns like a fire, drunk! Drunk in the embrace of the dancing girls, on the melodies of the jazz music, in the peach-colored wine glasses...

In the city of spring, the red makeup of the girls is even more delicate and beautiful, the tourists in the park are even more crowded, the music in the dance halls is even more intoxicating, and the pursuit of the opposite sex is even more frenzied!

Small Recipe

Four Kinds of Snacks

— Shang Zhen

"Life is all about eating," and besides, our country's culinary art is world-renowned, how can we not enjoy the blessings of the palate? However, bear paws and camel humps are not something ordinary people can afford. I've only heard of these two delicacies but never seen them. Let's just make some small snacks!

Kumquat Cakes: Select high-quality kumquats that are as plump as honey dates. Use a small knife to make incisions around the kumquat, with the distance between each cut about the length of a grain of rice. Too wide, and the seeds won't come out; too narrow, and it will break easily. After incising, squeeze out each seed, making the kumquat resemble a double-layered chrysanthemum, but be careful not to break it. Immediately put them in a clay pot with water and simmer over charcoal. When they're half-cooked, add white sugar, about twelve ounces of sugar for every pound of kumquats. Adding sugar will greatly increase the heat, so you must stir constantly, pressing each kumquat flat. Simmer until the kumquats turn from hard to soft and appear transparent, then immediately remove the pot from the heat. If the heat is too high, they will not only burn but also become stiff. Then, carefully pick out the translucent ones and place them in a glass jar, resembling golden flowers. When eaten, they are not only delicious and fragrant but also good for the stomach and spleen!

Magnolia Petals: Magnolias bloom in mid-spring, covering the trees in white. Pick the half-open ones, using only the middle layer of petals, as the outer layer is older and the inner part is bitter. Gently wash them with clean water; if they turn yellow from too much washing, they are no longer usable. Separately, mix glutinous rice flour (or fermented rice flour, though it tends to be a bit hard) with water and white sugar and set aside. Heat oil in a pot until boiling (the type of oil doesn't matter). Lightly clamp a petal with chopsticks, dip it fully in the flour mixture, and drop it into the pot. The heat should be gentle. When the edges appear slightly browned, remove them immediately. The magnolia petals are now ready. They taste fragrant, sweet, and crispy, leaving a pleasant lingering aroma in your mouth.

Rose Petal Jam: Place slightly ripe, not yet yellow, high-quality plums in a clay pot with some clean water. Simmer over charcoal until cooked through. Strain off the plum soup, as it will be too sour. Then, use chopsticks to remove the skin and pits and set them aside. Separately, prepare half-open rose blossoms. Remove the petals and discard the core. Mash the petals and squeeze out the juice. Then, combine them with white sugar (the amount of sugar should be about twice the weight of the plums; more flowers will result in a richer color) and mash together with the plum sauce from before and put into the pot. Simmer over charcoal until ready. The jam will have a bright color, strong fragrance, and fresh taste. Store it in a porcelain container for consumption at any time. You can also use salted plums, cleaned and combined with dried rose petals, but the results will be inferior in all aspects.

Purple Perilla Plums: Plums that are too small are tasteless, and those that are too ripe are not crispy. Therefore, use plump and crispy ones. Lightly crush them without removing the pits. Remove the old leaves or stems from the purple perilla that grows alongside the plums. Mix it with white sugar, using twice the weight of the plums. No need to simmer. Place them in a container and sun-dry for three to five days in the summer, turning them two or three times a day. Once the plum flesh has been dyed purple, they are ready to be chewed. They have a fragrant aroma, and their taste is far superior to the green plums sold in the market. The purple perilla is also delicious and has a unique flavor.

The above four items are snacks that the author's family often enjoys. They don't cost much, are hygienic, and have good color, aroma, and taste. I dare to offer them to the readers and ask the mistresses of the household, or those preparing to be, to try them out. If you only buy imported crackers or jams and give up the happiness of enjoying "national flavors," it is truly not worth it! Ah! How clean the air is, how refreshing to breathe! Those mountain views and waterscapes, fragrant flowers, and lush greenery are so much fun! The beauty of the scenery cannot be compared to even a fraction of what you can find in the dark and sunless city. Thus, one villa to the east, one mansion to the west, houses that blend Chinese and Western styles, are quickly being built.

Ah! After all, the countryside is dry and tasteless... Those clumsy, unkempt country bumpkins are really a bit annoying. It's hard to get a rickshaw, and my legs are killing me. The so-called entertainment is just a tea garden with incomplete doors and windows. "Damn it, let's go to the city!"

Oh! Those rental notices for the new houses are posted so big!

But, it's still so bustling...

"Revitalize the countryside!

Return to the countryside!"

Free Talk

Observations on "Ghost Writing"

— Wu Lou

There are many ghosts lurking in the literary world. Looking at it for a long time, one's physical eyes can transform into divine eyes. The beauty or ugliness of an article should be known at a glance. Like a skilled card player who knows what kind of card it is as soon as they touch it, experience creates a special feeling. The wonder of the divine eye is that one can casually sense what kind of person probably wrote a certain article, or what kind of article someone should write, as if seeing their liver and lungs.

The marvel is that one must first slightly distinguish between human and ghost. Some grand and majestic theories are ghost writings, while some that are not eye-catching are actually human writings. There are ghost writings that have not fully transformed into ghosts, and there are human writings that have already become ghostly. Among ghost writings, there are ghost writings with great supernatural powers, ghost writings with insufficient supernatural powers, and even honest little ghosts' ghost writings... and so on.

The era of telegraph seems to have passed. It's a pity that the death of a "Jiao Hanxiang" led to no more echoes. Some gentlemen cannot shake their heads and sway, and they are unhappy! That can be considered the most supernatural ghost writing. Then there was the era of declarations, the era of speeches, "Dear compatriots..." and other great works, which were still ghost writings. In addition, there are many social novels, which are even more like sketching shadows and are masterpieces in the ghost realm!

Anyone who has studied "logic" a little must know that there are many seemingly reasonable arguments that are actually based on wrong premises, or resounding articles that are far from the truth. For example, "To save the country, you must drink boiled water!" or "Great people must first gnaw on vegetable roots." These can only be classified as ghost talk, and there is no way to criticize them. Next are those that flash and sparkle, like magic tricks, with a wide variety of arguments, covering everything from ancient to modern, "Fried dough sticks and sesame cakes!" "National affairs are like playing chess!" Without a clear mind and sharp analysis, one will be confused by them. As for those who are twisted and affected, learning some slick and deceitful ways, making every effort to be cunning, and unable to justify themselves, these are the lowest of the low.

Those who are about to betray, their words are ashamed; those who are suspicious in their hearts, their words are rambling; the words of good people are few; the words of rash people are many; the words of those who slander good people are roving; the words of those who lose their integrity are submissive... The ancients also deeply understood how to read articles and listen to speeches. Many young people do not know the ways of the world, but they also know how to read articles, judge truth and falsehood, and distinguish between human and ghost. Where does that feeling come from? Could it be the light of a pure soul that can illuminate ghosts? In that case, where can all the deceivers and name-stealers of the past and present escape to?

Impressions of a Trip to Malaya

— Yue Ming

Traveling in a foreign country always seems to easily evoke foreign sentiments, but that was not the case on the train in the Federated Malay States. Almost all I saw along the way were Chinese compatriots, except for a few Malay ticket inspectors. Inside the carriage, upon entering, one sees the Chinese characters "Beware of Pickpockets." Arriving at a station, turning my head to look out the window, amidst the shoulders of the passengers, there was a sign with the place name in both Chinese and English. The rural thatched houses along the way were immediately eye-catching, but what stood out the most were the two strips of earthy red Spring Festival couplets pasted on the doors. The streets of the towns also flew by with many fabric signs covered in square characters.

"The prosperity of Malaya must be attributed to the Chinese!" I don't know whether I saw this sentence in some travelogue or in an essay in a Chinese newspaper. I had forgotten it completely, but now it re-entered my mind. I was sitting by the window, greedily taking in the Malay wilderness sleeping under the scorching sun.

The Malay wilderness under the scorching sun.

The person sitting next to me was noisily talking about business, and I occasionally heard a few despondent and resentful words.

"In the past, one could sell for one or two hundred dollars, but now, damn it, it's only worth ten or twenty dollars!"

I knew they were talking about rubber. Many people made fortunes from it during the European war. Now, with the world's economic panic, rubber prices have fallen sharply, and complaints are inevitable.

Almost all the mountains and fields along the way were man-made rubber forests, but some places showed an undisguised desolation. The people who collect the rubber sap were nowhere to be seen, and deep weeds grew at the foot of the trees. Occasionally, one could see ten miles of forest that had been burned bare, with charred tree trunks lying everywhere, like a battlefield. If some severed limbs were added, the distant traveler looking out the window would not be able to help but feel a sense of elegy, right? The train passed Kuala Lumpur, and a large group of Chinese compatriots got on, carrying simple luggage, saying they were going back to Guangdong. Their unclean clothes and melancholy faces surrounded me, reminding me of the ancient saying "return to one's hometown in wealth and honor," and my heart became as sad as theirs.

Your hands once prospered Malaya;

Your blood once fattened Malaya;

Now Malaya is weak and withered,

Go back, don't be nostalgic, don't be sad!

However, as the train rushed on into the night, when it reached Tank Road Station, the dancing Singapore, the singing Singapore, the drunken Singapore, surrounded me for a while and dazed me. I thought quietly;

"Malaya is still prosperous! I don't want to go back!"

But soon, like those compatriots, I returned to my country in sorrow. This was in the spring of 1931.

— Zang Kejia

I moved down, I moved down from that skyscraper made of stone, like an oriole leaving a tall tree, settling down in a bottomless valley.

In the high-rise, my heart couldn't bask in the sun. Looking at the sea waves, I slapped my suffocating chest,

A ghostly figure was nailed to my side, never letting go day or night. I closed this door, and the four walls all leaked radiance. A pair of black hands strangled the world, and here I breathe freely.

Inside and Outside the Bathroom (Continued)

— Jia Ming

"No, what do you mean..."

"I mean, let's go have some tea and snacks. Don't you have anything else to do?"

After taking a shower, I usually feel hungry. I agreed.

In the thick mist, I watched his plump back and plump legs disappear outside the bathroom door.

I gradually increased the warm water to the hottest temperature, showering it on my chest and back. I scrubbed the layers of my skin with force. When the heat became unbearable, I turned off the hot water and let the coldest water shower all over my body. After scrubbing thoroughly again, I slightly wiped myself with the small towel I had brought in and walked outside in my straw sandals.

I carefully looked for my friend and waited until a man in gray shorts standing in front of the mirror shouted loudly "Mr. Lu" to me before I recognized him.

He was combing his hair in front of the mirror, saying bits and pieces of things to me. He was wearing a gray short-sleeved shirt and shorts, and a pair of black cloth shoes.

For some reason, I felt a little scared. I looked closely at his face, that pair of thick eyebrows, the corners of his eyebrows seeming to reveal a fierce light, the short beard below, clearly hiding a cunning smile, a pair of small eyes, constantly sizing me up, as if with ill intentions. Just looking at his attire, he didn't seem like a good person at all.

I immediately regretted making the mistake of getting to know this friend. I remembered the story he had just told about the waiter stealing the guest's wallet, and I became even more flustered. I was afraid that this was a plan to attack from the east and strike from the west. I quietly felt my pockets while getting dressed and felt a little relieved when I found the fifty dollars was still there.

He was waiting next to me while I got dressed. I kept responding to him, but in my mind I was calculating how to find a way to get rid of him. He invited me to have tea together, and I thought this must be a trap.

After I finished dressing, we came out together. I pretended to need to tell my family, so I used the phone in the office to make a call.

I didn't dial the correct number. I held the phone, said questions and answers myself, pretending to listen, and then pretended to be surprised. Then I put down the receiver and told the person standing next to me that there was something important going on at my house, that I had to go back immediately, and I expressed my apologies for not being able to have tea with him.

I didn't hear clearly what he said in response. I quickly walked out onto the street, like a captured prisoner who had escaped. I immediately jumped into a rickshaw, pointed in the opposite direction from my house, and urged the rickshaw puller to hurry up and pull me away.

Sketches of Peiping (7) Night at the Crossroads

— Yao Ke

The market in Peiping closes much earlier than in Shanghai. Not to mention midwinter; even now that the weather is gradually warming up, the market still closes very early. For example, Wangfujing Street and the Dong'an Market area can be considered one of the most bustling areas in Peiping, but after nine or ten o'clock at night, it becomes deserted and sleeps in the curtain of night.

At this time, the crossroads outside Dong'an Market are only left with a few scattered passersby, a few rickshaws lazily waiting there. A few will-o'-the-wisp-like lights illuminate the food stalls – pancakes, pig's head meat, corn bread... faintly tempting the rickshaw pullers' appetite.

"Clang!" Four large copper coins fell from a skinny black hand onto a small stall. The stall owner quickly handed a "corn bread" to this black palm, which immediately went to a disheveled mouth with a short beard. "How about trying a piece of pig's head meat that was cooked today?"

"...Hai!" The short-bearded mouth swallowed the corn bread and began to speak. "...Don't mention it! After pulling all night, I only earned twenty coins (Note 1). How can that be enough to eat meat?"

"Eat first, we can settle up later. Isn't the Zhenguang Cinema about to close?" The stall owner casually handed over a piece of oily pig's head meat.

Dozens of cars and private cars were parked in front of the Zhenguang Cinema. There was still no movement at this time; their masters were still appreciating Greta Garbo's kissing poses, or drinking in Yang Xiaolou's "Picking the Curtain" at the Jixiang Theater to the west.

The pig's head meat had already entered his stomach, and his legs had to turn towards the entrance of Zhenguang Cinema to wait. After waiting for an hour with great difficulty, the movie finally ended, and men and women poured out from the door. Laughter, shouts, car horns, rickshaw pullers' throats – a chaotic symphony broke the dead air. But the people watching the movie were not crowded, and they all dispersed in a moment; the lively noise disappeared like light smoke, and the surrounding air blackly solidified into a团.

"Pao la!" (Note 2) A rough sound came from the short-bearded mouth. The black, thin hand listlessly dragged the rickshaw pole and turned back to the stall. "Pao la!"

"Wait for the Jixiang Theater to close." The stall owner's face showed a sympathetic bitter smile.

"Someone did hire me, but I didn't get the fare," the short-bearded man said, shaking his head. "To Baoguo Temple – such a long way – they only offered thirty coins! I said I don't want even a dime! Damn it! Pao la!"

The wind gradually picked up, carrying dust and cold, raging wildly at the crossroads. Jixiang Theater closed! Another burst of noise slowly subsided again. Seeing that the crowd was about to disperse, the short-bearded man still hadn't found an employer. "Pao la!" His heart was filled with anxiety.

"Rickshaw!" A person who came out last shouted. "Baoguo Temple."

"Two dimes."

"Twenty coins." As he spoke, the person only cared about walking west.

"One dime... Sir... It's twelve or thirteen miles..."

"Twenty-four coins." The person walked away. "Do you want forty coins?"

"Twenty-six coins."

"Pao la!" The rickshaw puller stared at the empty street, biting his teeth. Suddenly, he chased after him, shouting breathlessly... "I'll pull you for twenty-six coins!"

He pulled this twenty-six-coin employer, ran past the small stall where he had borrowed pig's head meat, and greeted the stall owner... "I'll give it to you tomorrow!" A few minutes later, the sound of his heavy footsteps faded away.

The night was deep. The crossroads were as silent as death.

(Note 1) Twenty coins are ten large copper coins, equivalent to four cents of silver.

(Note 2) "Pao la!" is Peiping rickshaw pullers' "slang," meaning similar to "it's over," or the Shanghai people's "dismantling the Old Immortal."

Journey

— Gongsun Min

The thin, old horse,

Carrying heavy luggage!

The man is on a journey.

The long whip urging the horse,

Tore through the dusk,

Drawing a faint trace of a new moon.

The swaying willow branches by the roadside,

Stir up the traveler's troubles;

Adding to the homesickness.

Looking at the drifting white clouds, who can know when they will return?

Thinking only increases sadness!

Let the evening wind blow

The thin clothes,

The weary traveler enters the deserted village.

"The fire is about to burn your eyebrows!"

Half a Day's Lessons (8)

— Li Huiying

I get angry whenever I think about this national anthem, saying that the 30 million people in the Northeast have "no suffering, no worries," and "no grievances." That can only deceive ghosts! Facts are the best eloquence. The 30 million people in the Northeast will not fall for your tricks and will not be anesthetized by you!

Next were speeches by many dignitaries, nothing more than deceitful nonsense. Then, amidst enthusiastic applause, the Japanese consul stood up to speak...

"I am honored to be able to participate in your country's grand event today! The reason is that these two anniversaries are very rare and have great significance in history.

"First, let's talk about September 18th. September 18th can be said to be the day when the Japanese Empire helped your country establish its foundation. The Empire has a relationship with Manchuria and Mongolia, being of the same culture and race, sharing the same fate, so it bravely withdrew from the League of Nations, regardless of other countries' complaints and accusations. Since the Empire initiated the establishment of your country, it must naturally recognize it afterward. Therefore, on this day last year, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent a document to your country's Ministry of Foreign Affairs, officially recognizing it. This is the origin of September 15th. When your people celebrate this grand event, they should remember the righteous act of the Empire in establishing your country. The two countries, Japan and Manchuria, must reach the stage of 'Japanese-Manchurian cooperation, co-existence, and co-prosperity'..."

After the speech, the Japanese elementary school students under the stage clapped and waved flags frantically. He calmly walked down the stage.

I don't know what others thought, but as for myself, I felt a chill and then a heat all over my body while listening to this speech. I had no other hope. I only hoped that I would suddenly turn into a bomb, causing everyone in the hall, both enemies and ourselves, to perish together!

I didn't know what other people were saying on the podium. I was too excited, I was too angry. But suddenly, a rumbling sound rang above my head. Two Japanese planes scattered a large number of leaflets from the sky. The crowd stirred, vying to pick up the falling pieces of paper. I grabbed one by the way, entitled "New Manchuria."

It was another long piece of sickening, deceptive talk.

The originally dull meeting place, due to the temporary commotion, seemed a bit more active. No, it would be better to say more scattered. In the student ranks, some were sitting on the ground, and some even tore off the small national flags and leaflets to wipe their snot. From their impatient looks, you could tell that everyone was hoping that this farce would end quickly so they could vent the depression in their chests.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Women and Careers

— Gu She

Some time ago, someone gave a speech at a girls' school, titled "Women and Careers." They said that the best career for women is to marry. This issue has sparked a lot of debate. I think this is exactly what that person meant by "humor." Which woman in today's society doesn't consider "marriage" as the only career? What about society, what about the country, it's all just empty talk. In the end, it's still about getting married. However, everyone is unwilling to say this fact out loud. When that person clearly stated it, everyone thought it was a strange idea. But in fact, that is precisely the current reality!

In fact, women today are indeed taking marriage as their only career. Whether it's pursuing education or engaging in social activities, in the end, it's still about getting married. Marriage is the destination for all women. Of course, of course, women should marry, and marriage is not a career, but now women's marriage is not for the sake of marriage, but for the sake of "having food and clothing." It's for the sake of a career. Don't you see? All the women who have married and become wives, who among them doesn't immediately break away from society? Except for those who go to movie theaters, dance halls, and all kinds of social gatherings, it's almost impossible to see them (of course, this refers to wealthy wives, and that person's speech was also addressed to wealthy women). This is clear evidence that women take marriage as their only career. Because at this point, they are already married and no longer need any social activities, and they are naturally guaranteed food and clothing. That is, they have already obtained a career now. The essence of why women take marriage as their only career lies in this.

However, is marriage really the best career for women? Of course not. This is just a temporary phenomenon that this society is exhibiting. Because women in this society are fundamentally appendages of men, and women have become a kind of commodity. That's why women can't help but take marriage as their only best career. If women can break away from the status of being appendages of men and liberate themselves from the status of wives to become people in society, then women will have no need to take marriage as their only best career. They will have independent abilities and opportunities for activity. They will be able to break through the shackles of money, step into the larger society, and become complete individuals. Of course, this is a matter for the future society.

And the realization of this future society depends on the efforts of women. Not only should women strive, but also male warriors who stand at the forefront of the times should also strive together. Originally, this is just one part of the solution to the entire social problem, and it is impossible to distinguish which comes first and which comes later, which is more important and which is less important; once the entire social problem is solved, everything will be solved. And in the meantime, women should work even harder for their own problems. Because this is a problem that concerns them directly.

Advanced women, pay attention to this issue! How to break free from the shackles of etiquette and money and become a person in society, this is something that everyone needs to carefully consider! You must know that "marriage is the only best career for women" is a disgrace! The greatest shame of modern women! How to fight out of this shame is the responsibility of the times for women!

A Day at Xinhua

— Dai Ni

I love music. I used to go to the Town Hall to listen to music with my English teacher, Miss Li. She plays the piano very well and thought that I, as her student, could at least play a little something like the胡琴. However, I am a complete amateur musician who can't even distinguish "Do Re Mi." She once curiously asked me, "What's the fun in listening if you don't understand?" My answer was that it's precisely because I don't understand that I like to listen to music. I also like to dance. When Black Cat was next to the 大光明, I used to go "to sit at a table" alone every night, listen to music, and watch people dance. When my friends found out, they would definitely force me to "go into the sea (dance)," so I dared not enter the dance hall. I thought watching people dance was very good, wasn't it? Because of this weird temperament that others recognized, I earned the nickname "lukewarm water." In fact, they don't understand me.

Yesterday, I was invited by Mr. Jin Peiyu to visit the Xinhua Opera Society, and I happily agreed. A night owl who doesn't know what the sun is actually got up at nine o'clock today. The intoxicating spring breeze brushed against my clothes, and our car headed towards善鐘路. I haven't seen the sun in years, and I haven't seen a spring morning in years. I leisurely felt like I was back in my childhood, flying a kite. I don't believe how a young man in his mid-twenties can seem like a dying old man!

I knocked on the door of No. 4 Meihua Lane, and all five fingers were stained black. I think it's a pity that Xinhua didn't put up a sign that the paint wasn't dry. As I stepped inside, Miss Zhang Wen, whom we (a familiar term for people from the same hometown) call "one two three four," was teaching····? It's dancing, just watching people dance. Because I was eager to go upstairs, I couldn't sit at a table and have a cup of coffee or tea. The men's dormitory is on the second floor; the women's, no, the young ladies' are on the third floor. All are wrought iron half-beds, white sheets and quilts, and colored pillowcases. If they practiced morning exercises in bed in the morning, I could introduce them to the director of sports films. This is a very beautiful new scene. Amateurs always like to talk like amateurs.

Recently, it seems that autograph books are very popular. I, an honest person who doesn't know how to be fashionable, also hid a small book and was kidnapping autographs everywhere. Naturally, this treasure trove,

Page 20

how could I easily let it go? Two young ladies' signatures are··· Don't let down your youth (Xu Jian)

Don't let down your golden age now (Yan Fei)

Thank you for reminding me. I don't even know that my youth exists anymore. I am heavily burdened by the burdens of life. I am a machine that lives for the sake of living. Youth, the golden age, have scattered like smoke in my life history. They will never have a day to return!

Retribution is clear, and the principles of heaven cycle. The small booklet was hidden in my pocket, and a beautiful "lai xie" (Mr. Yan Hua, this is Shanghainese) booklet was also placed in front of me. I think my original works are often buried in the wastepaper basket, which seems too bad, and now I can have the opportunity to write with a big brush. However, I think Mr. Yan Hua's is too boring (the writing is still very good). I want to change it···

I love to hear you say no to you,

Don't say··· "No!"

The title on the flyleaf of Mr. Zhu Jian (i.e., blowing bubbles) is···

Rely on your parents at home,

Rely on your friends when you're out.

There is Miss Fei Li, a niece of Ouyang Yuqian, she

allowed me (readers, don't misunderstand the meaning of this sentence) but didn't write a word. I am such a petty person. In order to get revenge, I will introduce her anecdote.

Everyone calls Miss Fei Li "standard nervous." It is said that after she "that" (this is a new pronoun), she almost went crazy for a day, and that "crazy" posture is enough to be called a "top-notch" (old lady, is that how these three words are written?) standard. This is the origin of the "standard nervous."

Now it's time to thank Mr. and Mrs. Yan Hua and all the members (the old lady was absent due to a hoarse voice. Someone asked me who the old lady was. I don't know, I'm afraid of getting nothing). Once we come to our Xin Sheng Radio Station to broadcast, you don't say that you sing really well. (Tan style) A large group of people came to the Oriental Hotel in a mighty manner because I love to hear you say no. Mr. Song Wei and Miss Ye Ying taught me. The amateur musician is really clever. I learned half of it in two hours. According to the direct proportion, will it be done in another two hours? Please pay attention to the date of the first audition. I guess it will definitely sound good when I sing. After you listen to it, don't say... no...!

In the evening, the old painter Ding Song, his wife, his son, etc. all came from the Biao Hotel and took away the old and young painter's paintings and calligraphy. I will remember this no matter what. Autograph, autograph. The father of Violet, one of the银汉双星, came to add to the fun with a comical song, a French-style performance, and a series of "pulis." The old man looked very happy, unlike because of the Queen's (the Emperor's wife) affairs, "that." (The origin of the new pronoun is here.) It's a pity that many people thought I knew him but didn't introduce him.

When my interest waned, it was already three o'clock. Because the iron gate of my house was closed, I lived alone in the hotel. After following Xinhua for a day, I couldn't fall asleep this time. Standing on the balcony, watching the sunrise, the sun did rise from the east. I saw it clearly. Poor friends who can't travel to famous places, I sincerely invite you to sit quietly on the sundeck (of course, you can't always lean on the balcony of the Oriental Hotel) before the sun comes out. At the very least, it's no less than watching the sunrise on Mount Tai.

Hiring a School Doctor

— Chen

A doctor friend who is also a classmate and fellow villager, Mr. Huimin, finally obtained a bachelor's degree four years ago after graduating from a national medical school.

It is possible to be frugal with eating and clothing, but when you get sick, you can't do without a doctor. With this bachelor's degree, even though he didn't study abroad, wouldn't he be a doctor? At that time, we all congratulated him like this.

In fact, this was just an ignorant view. After Huimin ended his golden student life, he felt the gap between the education system and the social organization, and was pushed into society as if he was walking into a deep marsh.

His increasingly bankrupt family had great hopes for him. Every year, they scrimped and saved, using most of their income to support his education without complaint. After graduation, they wanted Huimin to come to Shanghai to find a quiet and well-paid job that could not only support himself but also support his family. This was what Huimin's family hoped for.

Taking his family's hardships to heart, Huimin also ran out of school with this hope. However, the world is vast, like a boundless sea. Should he go to a hospital to seek a position? He had no connections, and no relatives to recommend him. Should he try to open a small clinic himself? He didn't have that kind of financial strength. Should he just go home? Not to mention that several years of hard study would be in vain, what was even more difficult was that he couldn't bear the ridicule of his fellow villagers and old acquaintances.

In this way, Huimin stumbled here and there, staying in this city, and for several years had not formally resolved his career, living a hungry and semi-unemployed life.

After several years of being whipped by life, Huimin's demands had been lowered from being a doctor and opening a clinic. It would also be good if he could teach at a school. One day, he saw an advertisement in the newspaper for hiring a school doctor, and he ran to contact them with such hope.

Enduring a kind of contemptuous questioning from the doorman, Huimin was led into a room that served as both a teachers' lounge and an office. After the doorman reported the visitor's intention to the administrative director, he withdrew. The administrative director said "please sit down" and used his eyes to size up this new guest.

"What is your surname, sir?" the host asked.

"The surname is..."

"Where are you from?"

"...Province."

"Which school did you attend before...?"

"Graduated from a medical school." Huimin felt like a prisoner being interrogated in court, feeling uneasy and ashamed.

"Ah, that's very good..." The administrative director narrowed his eyes and continued, "However, the school doctor's job at our school is very troublesome. There are many students, and I'm afraid you, sir..."

"That doesn't matter. Please tell me about your school's situation."

"We have a total of four schools, including the middle school and the elementary school, with a total of more than 800 people. We hold office twice a week, once for three hours, and additionally..."

"Four schools?"

"That's right, four schools share one school doctor. Additionally, there are two hours of physiology and hygiene at this school."

After listening to the administrative director's words, Huimin thought to himself that six hours per school every week, four times six is twenty-four hours, plus two hours of teaching, a total of twenty-six hours, which already exceeds the teaching time of all middle school teachers. At the same time, given the large number of people and the scattered locations of the schools, how would he have enough time? But it's better than being idle, so he asked:

"There are so many people, and they're not all in one place. I'm afraid it will be difficult for the students..."

"That's nothing. Anyway, it's just checking their bodies every semester and looking at them every week. Would the school really become a hospital?... Haha..." The administrative director's laugh was meaningful.

"In that case, what is your school's compensation...?" the guest asked.

"This needs to be discussed. Our school can only... can only offer 40 yuan per semester because of financial difficulties." The administrative director's face suddenly turned very stern.

The guest just stared at the other person in a daze.

"This is naturally only considered a subsidy for pocket money. Sir, when you are willing, it is entirely of a voluntary nature."

"Ah! Of a voluntary nature."

Huimin suddenly understood in his heart. He said goodbye and came out. In the small courtyard behind him, the students were noisily shouting.
